create table entertainment (
        ShowID            int,
        Title             varchar(500), 
        DateAdded         varchar(20), 
        ReleaseYear       int,          
        Rating            varchar(10),
        Description       varchar(500), 
        EntertainmentType char(10), 
    primary key (ShowID)
) ;

INSERT INTO entertainment
(ShowID, Title, DateAdded, ReleaseYear, EntertainmentType, Description, Rating)
VALUES


create table entertainmentgenre  (
        ShowID         int,
        GenreType      varchar(30),
    primary key (ShowID, GenreType),
    foreign key (ShowID) references entertainment (ShowID)
) ;

create table entertainmentDirector  (
        ShowID         int,
        DirectorName   varchar(50) NOT NULL,
    primary key (ShowID, DirectorName),
    foreign key (ShowID) references entertainment (ShowID)
) ;

create table entertainmentCast(
        ShowID         int,
        CastName      varchar(50) not null,
    primary key (ShowID, CastName),
    foreign key (ShowID) references entertainment (ShowID)
) ;

create table producedIn(
        ShowID         int,
        CountryName      varchar(30) not null,
    primary key (ShowID, CountryName),
    foreign key (ShowID) references entertainment (ShowID)
) ;
